time.Now()\n\tmetricImageSizeBytes.WithLabelValues(\"input\").Observe(float64(len(data)))\n\tdefer func() { getImageProcessingMetrics().Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds(), 1, &err, \"process\") }()\n\n\tdecoded, format, err := image.Decode(bytes.NewReader(data))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, \"\", errors.Wrap(err, \"failed to decode img\")\n\t}\n\n\tbounds := decoded.Bounds()\n\twidth, height := bounds.Dx(), bounds.Dy()\n\n\tlongest := max(width, height)\n\ttotalPixels := width * height\n\tmaxPixels := int(MaxMegaPixels * 1_000_000)\n\n\tneedsResize := longest > MaxImageDimension || totalPixels > maxPixels\n\tneedsCompress := len(data) > MaxCompressedSize\n\tif !needsResize && !needsCompress {\n\t\tmetricImageSizeBytes.WithLabelValues(\"output\").Observe(float64(len(data)))\n\t\treturn data, mediaType, nil\n\t}\n\n\tif needsResize {\n\t\t// Fit within MaxImageDimension while preserving aspect ratio\n\t\tdecoded = fitImage(decoded, MaxImageDimension, MaxImageDimension)\n\n\t\t// Further scale if still over megapixel limit\n\t\tbounds := decoded.Bounds()\n\t\tif bounds.Dx()*bounds.Dy() > maxPixels {\n\t\t\tscale := math.Sqrt(float64(maxPixels) / float64(bounds.Dx()*bounds.Dy()))\n\t\t\tnewWidth := int(float64(bounds.Dx()) * scale)\n\t\t\tnewHeight := int(float64(bounds.Dy()) * scale)\n\t\t\tdecoded = transform.Resize(decoded, newWidth, newHeight, transform.MitchellNetravali)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tresult, outputType, err = encodeWithSizeLimit(decoded, format)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, \"\", err\n\t}\n\tmetricImageSizeBytes.WithLabelValues(\"output\").Observe(float64(len(result)))\n\n\treturn result, outputType, nil\n}\n\n// fitImage resizes an image to fit within maxWidth x maxHeight while preserving aspect ratio.\n// If the image already fits, it is returned unchanged.\nfunc fitImage(img image.Image, maxWidth, maxHeight int) image.Image {\n\tbounds := img.Bounds()\n\twidth, height := bounds.Dx(), bounds.Dy()\n\n\tif width <= maxWidth && height <= maxHeight {\n\t\treturn img\n\t}\n\n\t// Calculate scale factor to fit within bounds\n\tscaleW := float64(maxWidth) / float64(width)\n\tscaleH := float64(maxHeight) / float64(height)\n\tscale := math.Min(scaleW, scaleH)\n\n\tnewWidth := int(float64(width) * scale)\n\tnewHeight := int(float64(height) * scale)\n\n\treturn transform.Resize(img, newWidth, newHeight, transform.MitchellNetravali)\n}\n\n// encodeWithSizeLimit encodes an image, reducing JPEG quality until under MaxCompressedSize.\n// PNGs that exceed the limit are converted to JPEG.\nfunc encodeWithSizeLimit(img image.Image, format string) ([]byte, string, error) {\n\tbounds := img.Bounds()\n\tpixels := bounds.Dx() * bounds.Dy()\n\n\tisPNG := format == \"png\"\n\n\t// Only try PNG for small images - large PNGs won't fit under MaxCompressedSize\n\tif isPNG && pixels <= pngSizeThreshold {\n\t\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\t\tif err := png.Encode(&buf, img); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, \"\", errors.Wrap(err, \"failed to encode PNG\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif buf.Len() <= MaxCompressedSize {\n\t\t\tmetricImageEncoding.WithLabelValues(format, \"png\").Inc()\n\t\t\treturn buf.Bytes(), \"image/png\", nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Encode as JPEG, reducing quality until under size limit\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\tfor _, quality := range jpegQualities {\n\t\tbuf.Reset()\n\t\tif err := jpeg.Encode(&buf, img, &jpeg.Options{Quality: quality}); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, \"\", errors.Wrap(err, \"failed to encode JPEG\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif buf.Len() <= MaxCompressedSize {\n\t\t\tmetricImageEncoding.WithLabelValues(format, \"jpeg\").Inc()\n\t\t\treturn buf.Bytes(), \"image/jpeg\", nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil, \"\", errors.Newf(\"image too large: %d bytes after compression (max %d)\", buf.Len(), MaxCompressedSize)\n}\n","numLines":187,"startLine":1,"totalLines":187}}}
